           `#q6` to `#q4` is NOT present as `(move_base #q6 #q4 #o0)`. Instead I see `(move_base #q6 #q4 #o0)`. The `o0` should be a trajectory, not a continuous parameter. The valid actions show `btraj(#t...)`. So the trajectory needs to be a specific instance.
